\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Synchronous serial channel driver for S\+P\+I-\/like communication. 

The S\+PI driver uses Universal Serial Interface Channel(\+U\+S\+I\+C) module. The U\+S\+IC module supports multiple data lines for S\+PI communication. ~\newline

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Full duplex communication with 2 separate lines for transmission and reception.
\item Half duplex communication with 1 common line shared for transmission and reception.
\item Dual mode communication with 2 common lines shared for transmission and reception.
\item Quad mode communication with 4 common lines shared for transmission and reception.~\newline
~\newline

\end{DoxyEnumerate}

S\+PI driver provides structures, enumerations and A\+P\+Is for configuring the U\+S\+IC channel for S\+PI communication and also for data transaction.~\newline
 S\+PI driver features\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Configuration structure X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+t and S\+PI initialization function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}}
\item Allows configuration of protocol word and frame length using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga16ee7fa348155fd43fc58c18787110db}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Word\+Length()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga52e6177c2885b2456cacbc26d2eaaaae}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Length()}}
\item Allows manipulation of data frame at runtime using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga58e79222d22c33f9713bb687f8fef155}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+S\+O\+F()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga097338770a47e3995056da8f82e9bd41}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+E\+O\+F()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga065897e36db1bbcffe141ad992cea9ce}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Slave\+Select()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga5b2480876aa7c3b1c9646156d015e398}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Slave\+Select()}}
\item Provides A\+P\+Is for transmitting data and receiving data using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga273573d7d388e93ff9018ff87abe9dc0}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Transmit()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga0ee3b6409eebaf1795632bf5a578b98c}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Receive()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga55ae75a9f812ee0ed92303074e990f97}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Get\+Received\+Data()}}
\item Allows configuration of shift clock using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga334e734eca67e44d05d82c195bf08e85}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Configure\+Shift\+Clock\+Output()}}
\item Provides enumeration of S\+PI protocol events using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gab7bf135472a433021877a83918680b21}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t}} 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Clear\+Status\+Flag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{flag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address. \\
\hline
{\em flag} & Protocol event status to be cleared for detection of next occurence. Refer @ X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t for valid values. {\bfseries{OR}} combinations of these enum item can be used as input. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Clears the events specified, by setting P\+S\+CR register.~\newline
~\newline
During communication the events occurred have to be cleared to detect their next occurence.~\newline
e.\+g\+: During transmission Transmit buffer event occurs to indicating data word transfer has started. This event has to be cleared after transmission of each data word. Otherwise next event cannot be recognized.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Configure\+Shift\+Clock\+Output (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga343d8f2c1d23c1fdf78a8251ece89e6d}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+B\+R\+G\+\_\+\+S\+H\+I\+F\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+P\+A\+S\+S\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+t}}}]{passive\+\_\+level,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gaf71e5e99d043dc33f3681e65f87c7cc8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+B\+R\+G\+\_\+\+S\+H\+I\+F\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+t}}}]{clock\+\_\+output }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address. \\
\hline
{\em passive\+\_\+level} & polarity and delay of the selected shift clock.~\newline
 Refer \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga343d8f2c1d23c1fdf78a8251ece89e6d}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+B\+R\+G\+\_\+\+S\+H\+I\+F\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+P\+A\+S\+S\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+t}} for valid inputs. \\
\hline
{\em clock\+\_\+output} & shift clock source.~\newline
 Refer \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gaf71e5e99d043dc33f3681e65f87c7cc8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+B\+R\+G\+\_\+\+S\+H\+I\+F\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+t}} for valid inputs.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Configures the shift clock source with the selected polarity and delay by setting B\+R\+G.\+S\+C\+L\+K\+O\+S\+EL and B\+R\+G.\+S\+C\+L\+K\+C\+FG.~\newline
~\newline
In Master mode operation, shift clock is generated by the internal baud rate generator. This S\+C\+LK is made available for external slave devices by S\+C\+L\+K\+O\+UT signal.~\newline
In Slave mode, the signal is received from the external master. So the D\+X1(input) stage has to be connected to input.~\newline
The shift clock output(\+S\+C\+L\+K\+O\+U\+T) signal polarity can be set relative to S\+C\+LK, with the delay of half the shift clock period. These settings are applicable only in master mode. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Use this function in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gaf6045fb4fe2d7199b2585e5d3d0f5957}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Data\+Transmission()}} to fill the F\+I\+FO and send the F\+I\+FO content without gaps in the transmission. F\+I\+FO is filled using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gacc0a4521925fd852e7e08075235d85fb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+X\+F\+I\+F\+O\+\_\+\+Put\+Data()}}.

Configure to disable the M\+S\+L\+S(\+Slave select signal) if the current data frame is considered as finished, by setting P\+C\+R.\+F\+EM bit.~\newline
~\newline

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Enable data transmission.~\newline
~\newline
Use this function in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga68e176cf5b557f8be0af0fb1398d45e6}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Data\+Transmission()}} to fill the F\+I\+FO and send the F\+I\+FO content without gaps in the transmission. F\+I\+FO is filled using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gacc0a4521925fd852e7e08075235d85fb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+X\+F\+I\+F\+O\+\_\+\+Put\+Data()}}. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you need more control over the start of transmission use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_ga04c66a47ae22c847b394f10d85e01bf8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Start\+Transmision\+Mode()}}
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{SPI@{SPI}!XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF@{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF}}
\index{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF@{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF}!SPI@{SPI}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF()}{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableEOF()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+E\+OF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Configure the handling of end of frame through software, by setting T\+C\+S\+R.\+E\+OF bit.~\newline
~\newline
This can be used if the software handles the T\+B\+UF data without F\+I\+FO. If E\+OF is set, a valid content of the T\+B\+UF is considered as last word of a frame. After transfer of the last word, M\+S\+LS signal becomes inactive. For software handling of E\+OF bit, it is recommended to configure T\+C\+S\+R.\+W\+L\+E\+MD as 0. ~\newline
{\bfseries{Note\+:}} The A\+PI should be called before putting the last data word of the frame to T\+B\+UF.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga2cd6466b19d02c7db01a55eaca7d2a73}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+E\+O\+F()}} 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableFEM()}{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableFEM()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+F\+EM (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
Configure to keep M\+S\+L\+S(\+Slave select signal) active even after finishing the current data frame, by setting P\+C\+R.\+F\+EM bit.~\newline
~\newline
This is typically used during the transmission of multi-\/data word frames, where there is possibility of delay in delivering the data. Frame end mode is enabled in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}} during initialization. To disable \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga064bf59979eafc6d8db3469a8e5b5e09}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+F\+E\+M()}} can be invoked as needed in the program.

\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Input\+Inversion (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga53c070bf62400b04864cb8409ffb17e9}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+t}}}]{input }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address. \\
\hline
{\em input} & S\+PI channel input stage.~\newline
 Refer \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga53c070bf62400b04864cb8409ffb17e9}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+t}} for valid inputs.\\
\hline

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Enables the polarity inversion of input data signal, by setting D\+Xy\+C\+R.\+D\+P\+OL(where y = {\itshape input}).~\newline
~\newline
This is not set in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}}. Invoke \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga564d521ad28281f2476c7e396b9c0e7a}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Input\+Inversion()}} as needed later in the program. To disable the inversion \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga78b13095d98676f05156650416d8d7ea}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Input\+Inversion()}} can be invoked.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\index{SPI@{SPI}!XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay@{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay}}
\index{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay@{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay}!SPI@{SPI}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay()}{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_EnableInterwordDelay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Interword\+Delay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Enables the delay after each word, by setting P\+C\+R.\+T\+I\+W\+EN bit.~\newline
~\newline
The inter word delay starts at the end of last S\+C\+LK cycle of data word. During this time no clock pulses are generated and M\+S\+LS signal stays active. If inter word delay is not enabled, last data bit of a data word is directly followed by the first data bit of the next data word. This is not enabled in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}}. To enable \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga59ee330dd7a2067e9787c70895dfbe24}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Interword\+Delay()}} has to be invoked as needed in the program. And can be disabled by invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gafc6069173601890ece01f79d941a9253}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Interword\+Delay()}}.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gafc6069173601890ece01f79d941a9253}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Interword\+Delay()}} 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Enables the generation of Master clock by setting P\+C\+R.\+M\+C\+LK bit.~\newline
~\newline
This clock can be used as a clock reference for external devices. This is not enabled during initialization in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}}. Invoke \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga9e7a909086914cc4a1afd1d51d2426ce}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Master\+Clock()}} to enable as needed in the program, or if it is disabled by \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gac5d22f078ebfcf9fd0950ba200916dda}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Master\+Clock()}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+S\+OF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Configure the handling of start of frame through software, by setting T\+C\+S\+R.\+S\+OF bit.~\newline
~\newline
This can be used if the software handles the T\+B\+UF data without F\+I\+FO. If S\+OF is set, a valid content of the T\+B\+UF is considered as first word of a new frame by finishing the currently running frame. For software handling of S\+OF bit, it is recommended to configure T\+C\+S\+R.\+W\+L\+E\+MD as 0. This is not configured during initialization. \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga58e79222d22c33f9713bb687f8fef155}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+S\+O\+F()}} can be called as needed in the program and can be disabled by \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gaeb14a87d61acd28815613659045786f0}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+S\+O\+F()}}.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

 Refer data structure \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gac7b5f3104f5bc43ce8c3ca4f3447f0c4}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+t}} for detail.\\

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Initializes the selected S\+PI {\itshape channel} with the {\itshape config} structure.~\newline
~\newline
Enable S\+PI channel by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_ga0567321036170adb335fef9b36dc3b71}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable()}} and then configures 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Baudrate, 
\item Passive data level as active high, 
\item Shift control signal as active high, 
\item Frame length as 64U, 
\item Word length as 8U, 
\item Enable Hardware port control mode, 
\item Enable transmission of data T\+D\+V(\+Transmit data valid) bit is set to 1, 
\item Enable invalidation of data in T\+B\+UF once loaded into shift register, 
\item Parity mode settings 
\end{DoxyItemize}And if master mode is selected, 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Enables M\+S\+LS signal generation, 
\item configures slave selection as normal mode, 
\item Set polarity for the Slave signal, 
\item Enable Frame end mode(\+M\+S\+L\+S signal is kept active after transmission of a frame) 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the interrupt node for U\+S\+IC channel events. ~\newline
~\newline
For an event to generate interrupt, node pointer should be configured with service request(S\+R0, S\+R1..S\+R5). The N\+V\+IC node gets linked to the interrupt event by doing so.~\newline
 Note\+: N\+V\+IC node should be separately enabled to generate the interrupt.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Length (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t}]{frame\+\_\+length }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\em frame\+\_\+length} & Number of bits in a frame. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} 1 to 64. If the value 64 is configured, then the frame does not automatically end. User should explicitly end the frame.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Define the data frame length.~\newline
~\newline
Set the number of bits to be serially transmitted in a frame. The frame length should be multiples of word length. If the value is set to 64, the frame does not automatically end. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga5b2480876aa7c3b1c9646156d015e398}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Slave\+Select()}} to end the frame after all the data is transmitted.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Selects the data source for S\+PI input stage, by configuring D\+X\+C\+R.\+D\+S\+EL bits.~\newline
~\newline
Selects the input data signal source among D\+XnA, D\+XnB.. D\+XnG for the input stage. The A\+PI can be used for all the input stages like D\+X0\+CR, D\+X1\+CR etc. This is not done during initialization. This has to be configured before starting the S\+PI communication. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Interrupt\+Node\+Pointer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t}]{service\+\_\+request }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the interrupt node for S\+PI channel events.~\newline
~\newline
For an event to generate interrupt, node pointer should be configured with service request(S\+R0, S\+R1..S\+R5). The N\+V\+IC node gets linked to the interrupt event by doing so. This is not configured in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}} during initialization.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Note\+::}

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item N\+V\+IC node should be separately enabled to generate the interrupt.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_SetInterwordDelay()}{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_SetInterwordDelay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Interword\+Delay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{tinterword\+\_\+delay\+\_\+ns }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address. \\
\hline
{\em tinterword\+\_\+delay\+\_\+ns} & delay in terms of nano seconds.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Configures the inter word delay by setting P\+C\+R.\+P\+C\+T\+Q1, P\+C\+R.\+D\+C\+T\+Q1 bit fields.~\newline
~\newline
The inter word delay is dependent on the peripheral clock. The maximum possible value is calculated by using the below formula~\newline
 Maximum inter word delay = ((1 + P\+C\+T\+Q1\+\_\+max)(1 + D\+C\+T\+Q1\+\_\+max)) / peripheral clock~\newline
 where P\+C\+T\+Q1\+\_\+max = 3 and D\+C\+T\+Q1\+\_\+max = 31~\newline
After configuring the inter word delay, this has to be enabled by invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga59ee330dd7a2067e9787c70895dfbe24}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Interword\+Delay()}}.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga59ee330dd7a2067e9787c70895dfbe24}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Enable\+Interword\+Delay()}},\mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gace30f648b7f55f3c4c7fe9ad78fa3f34}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Interword\+Delay\+S\+C\+L\+K()}} 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Set the selected U\+S\+IC channel to operate in S\+PI mode, by setting C\+C\+R.\+M\+O\+DE bits.~\newline
~\newline
It should be executed after \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}} during initialization. By invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga7fd532dae41a2b9d754aa3de0f412a8d}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Stop()}}, the M\+O\+DE is set to I\+D\+LE state. Call \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gacc7f1ad4ff8a6ae93bd2a466656ad864}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Start()}} to set the S\+PI mode again, as needed later in the program.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_Transmit()}{XMC\_SPI\_CH\_Transmit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Transmit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const uint16\+\_\+t}]{data,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gad590d901ed01f4b5a196542efc34e576}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+t}}}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & A constant pointer to X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t, pointing to the U\+S\+IC channel base address. \\
\hline
{\em data} & Data to be transmitted \\
\hline
{\em mode} & Communication mode of the S\+PI, based on this mode T\+C\+I(\+Transmit control information)is updated.~\newline
 Refer \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_gad590d901ed01f4b5a196542efc34e576}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+t}} for valid values.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Puts the data into F\+I\+FO, if F\+I\+FO mode is enabled or else into standard buffer, by setting the proper mode.~\newline
~\newline
In Dual and Quad modes, hardware port control(C\+C\+R.\+H\+P\+C\+EN) mode is enabled. By enabling this the direction of the data pin is updated by hardware itself. T\+C\+I(\+Transmit Control Information) allows dynamic control of both the data shift mode and pin direction during data transfers by writing to S\+C\+T\+R.\+D\+SM and S\+C\+T\+R.\+H\+P\+C\+D\+IR bit fields. To support this auto update, T\+C\+S\+R.\+H\+P\+C\+M\+D(\+Hardware Port control) will be enabled during the initialization using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_p_i_ga8b16f43a349603e746885a6d0d00b312}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+S\+P\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}} for all modes.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
